<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">威力值：</font><font face="宋体">8</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">B+2000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：自由动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font><font face="宋体">5点道力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">成分：姿势、言语、材料</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：自身</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：立即</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：就在这时，一道青色的波纹忽然扩散开来，将大半个塌陷处笼罩其中</font><font face="宋体">!</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">“坎术为末，水中花!”</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">她的坠落速度瞬间慢了下来</font><font face="宋体">,</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">不止如此，连那些石头掉落的景象，也变得清晰可辨，仿佛周围的一切物体都被无形之水裹住，行迹速度大为减缓。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">唯独不变的只有施术者</font><font face="宋体">——方先道。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">她惊讶的看到，方先道以流畅的步伐穿梭于落石碎木之间，同时向她射出一张符篆。当那张符纸正中她的额头时，青色波纹对她的影响也骤然消失。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：该法术每个场景只能发动一次。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">施展后，你立即获得</font><font face="宋体">3个移动动作，这段时间内对于其他生物来说是完全静止的，你可以如常使用动作。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">在法术持续期间内，如果你的任何行为或者与你相关的任何行动（如你的召唤物，投影，持续性效果）影响到其他生物（包括该生物身上的状态，他的召唤物，不属于你的物品等），则本效果立即结束，你失去本法术带来的未使用的一切动作。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">同时，若你使用本法术后，移动距离超过</font><font face="宋体">1000米，则本法术持续时间也会立即停止。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊：本法术并非时间带来的效果，面对免疫时间效果影响的目标，你依然可以如常发动本效果，其不会因为你多出来的回合与你一起行动。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：</font><font face="宋体">“艮术归申——不动明神！”</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">文行远拿出了自己压箱底的绝技，此术乃枢密府高等秘传，能大幅提高方士的力量、抵御力，可谓凡躯仙体、刀枪不入。练到高深处，甚至能召唤明王虚影为自己而战。虽然他修炼至今也未能完全参悟此法，但至少能发挥出护身功效，挡下几次刀砍剑劈不成问题。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">接着他借助明神之威，一个箭步朝面具男冲去，双拳直击对方的胸口！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">想要退，必先进！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你获得</font><font face="宋体">12点天生防御，获得4点全伤害吸收。你可以进行近战施法攻击，并且你的近战攻击检定获得12DP能量加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">在面对解除魔法，打断法术等类似效果时，本法术不判定为法术。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">增幅：你每有</font><font face="宋体">1点传奇决心，就可以额外消耗3点道力，再获得6点天生防御。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">成分：姿势、言语、材料（一件白刃武器）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：以自身为中心</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：所有目标（不分敌我，不包括自己）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：半径为智力值</font><font face="宋体">*10米的锥形</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：立即</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：</font><font face="宋体">“那就试一试好了！”百展高喝一声，手中的长剑仿佛化成无数剑影，“坤术为巳，斩无垠！”</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">刹那间，由剑刃构成的风暴完全吞没了羽衣所站立的位置</font><font face="宋体">——不光是干和雨玲珑，连这栋屋子的墙壁与房顶，都被千百道剑光同时斩中！木屑和瓦砾到处飞溅，剑身碰撞所绽放出的火光络绎不绝。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">哪怕是干，恢复能力也是有极限的！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">只要他护着雨玲珑不敢动弹，迟早会被此剑斩成碎片！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：本法术不会导致施法材料被消耗。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你使用该法术时，若该武器拥有当你进行近战白刃攻击时才能生效的特性，则在使用该法术时也能生效。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你进行一次施法检定，对范围内的所有目标造成相当于你（武器伤害</font><font face="宋体">+威力值）点的范围伤害，伤害类型与伤害级别与原本的武器伤害相同，并且获得武器的所有特性。所有受影响的目标反射豁免，但是其豁免检定失去相当于你施法检定成功数/点减值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">增幅：你每有</font><font face="宋体">1点传奇决心，就可以额外消耗5点道力，令本法术的威力值增加4点，施法检定获得6DP能量加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">威力值：</font><font face="宋体">8</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">B+2000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：标准动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font><font face="宋体">5点道力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">成分：姿势、言语</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：智力值</font><font face="宋体">*5米，确定正方形四角的一个点</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：所有目标（不分敌我，不包括自己）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：边长为智力值</font><font face="宋体">*米的正方形</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：需引导，引导无需动作，最大可持续一场景</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：颜箐此刻低吟出声。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">“坤术为巳，星罗地网！”</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">随着她话音落地，数不清的锁链冲天而起，像锚索一样朝着周边的墙壁扎去！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">它们并非笔直射出，而是互相交错，组成了成百上千道</font><font face="宋体">“链墙”。从远处望去，仿佛整个洞穴空间都被这些锁链布满，并分隔成了无数三尺见方的方格！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你进行一次施法检定，记录成功数，然后，在持续时间内，该法术范围内的目标发起移动时，你可以令其受到成功数点</font><font face="宋体">/穿刺严重伤害、剧痛点数和纠缠点数。伤害强韧豁免，剧痛点数意志豁免，纠缠点数强韧豁免，剧痛点数和纠缠点数均可以叠加。一个目标在一轮内最多只会受到该效果影响一次。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">并且你对该法术范围内的目标，你视为拥有颤动感知，这表现为，你的锁链布满了该范围内的所有空间。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===========================================================================================================

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：标准动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font><font face="宋体">5点道力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">成分：姿势、言语、材料（墓穴花瓣和蛆虫干）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：智力值</font><font face="宋体">*5米</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：一个目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：立即</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：负责人更是神情大变</font><font face="宋体">,摸出一小簇墓穴花瓣与蛆虫干，抬手甩向镇守!</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这是乾术腐生的起手式，对付坤属和坎属类的敌人有奇效</font><font face="宋体">,就算对方心性再坚定,也抵挡不住腐败的侵蚀,一旦中了,至少也得丧失好一会作战能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">然而对方没躲没避反倒从袖子里摸出几个青铜方块。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">乾术精准地命中了位于台阶中部的</font><font face="宋体">“镇守",他裸露在外的皮肤快速变得苍白,接着开始腐坏、脱落。按理说,此过程会带来巨大的痛苦,但他却没有太多反应,依旧坚持将青铜方块抛向操纵仙器的众人。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你对目标进行一次远程施法攻击，本次攻击检定获得</font><font face="宋体">6DP能量加值，造成毒素严重伤害，并令目标获得等同于造成伤害点数的剧痛点数，强韧豁免，可以叠加。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">增幅：你每有</font><font face="宋体">1点传奇决心，就可以额外消耗3点道力，令本次攻击检定获得6DP能量加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===========================================================================================================

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">坎术</font><font face="宋体">·引神魂</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">专业：道术</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">威力值：</font><font face="宋体">8</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">B+2000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：标准动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font><font face="宋体">5点道力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：智力值</font><font face="宋体">*5米</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：一个目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：</font><font face="宋体">24小时</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：</font><font face="宋体">“坎术为卯，引神魂！”</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">刹那间，夏凡感到自己坠入了她的眼眸之中</font><font face="宋体">——那是一片深不见底的浩海，无数色彩扑面而来，他仿佛看到了神经与髓鞘构成的拓扑网，又好似瞧见了气组成的漫天星辰。当一切异象重新聚拢成金色的瞳孔时，他才发觉自己仍留在原地。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你进行心灵检定，本次心灵检定可以获得相当于威力值</font><font face="宋体">/点招式加值，目标意志豁免。若成功，则你可以在目标意识内种下一个楔子。然后在持续时间内，当目标进行自己的回合时，你可以无需动作发动该法术，控制目标执行一个标准动作，然后持续时间立刻结束。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这是一个</font><font face="宋体">B级影响心灵效果，也是一个幻觉效果。拥有任何一项免疫的能力，则可以无视本效果。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">针对一个目标，你</font><font face="宋体">24小时之内只能对该目标施展一次本能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">在持续时间结束前，你无法再次发动该能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊的，若目标意志豁免对抗失败，则其本身不会发现你对其使用了该法术。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：需引导，引导无需动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：到头来终得看自己。石方士面沉如水，催动体内的气朝洛轻轻虚抓，</font><font face="宋体">“坤术为巳，蟒绞！”</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这是他赖以成名多年的杀招。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">在数百次搏杀中，他用这一手坤术绞死过相当于百刃水平的敌人，纹刻在皮肤上的符印可以令他不需要药引也能施展出颇具杀伤力的二重术。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">但最让他引以为豪的，是对蟒绞术的改进。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">基础秘录中，此术需要抓住对手才能起效，而他却将距离延伸了出去，宛如一条真正的</font><font face="宋体">“无形巨蟒”，甚至能隔墙杀人。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">快速、隐蔽、被困住后难以呼救，刺杀时悄无声息，皆是他深受娘娘器重的原因。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你以施法检定对目标发起擒抱，当其发起挣脱检定时，你也用施法检定对抗。若成功擒抱，则在被擒抱期间，目标也进入沉默和窒息状态。仅在计算该技能造成的擒抱时，你的触及改为智力值</font><font face="宋体">*5米。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">=========================================================================================================== 
  </font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">艮术</font><font face="宋体">·向圣山</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">关键字：【地】</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">威力值：</font><font face="宋体">8</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：移动动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font><font face="宋体">5点道力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">成分：姿势、言语、材料（一个石制雕像）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：智力值</font><font face="宋体">*5米</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：见下</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：见下</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：</font><font face="宋体">1分钟</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：古尔察一把扯开自己的头盔，令自己暴露在灼热的空气中。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">“喝！艮术为辰，向圣山！”</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">随着他的话音落地，露台的地面突然</font><font face="宋体">“活”了起来，十几个类似尊者的魁梧人形从蠕动的岩石中钻出，如山墙一般挡在了邪祟面前。这些人形双手合十，并不主动进攻邪祟，仿佛只是虔诚的祈求者。但任何一只邪祟只要碰到这些泥像，便会瞬间被沙砾石块吞噬，成为祈祷者的一部分！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这个术法已经和阵术无异！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">在对付感气者时，它或许不够灵活，可在大规模阵战与对付邪祟集群时，它的效果却极为醒目！敌人越多，就越容易深陷其中，术法中央的</font><font face="宋体">“圣山”，则是敌人可望而不可及的神圣之地。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你召唤智力值</font><font face="宋体">/个泥像，泥像不能直接出现在其他目标的位置上，每个泥像所占据的位置都是一格，泥像不能移动，当有目标进入到一个泥像所在的位置时，其获得你的智力值/点晶化点数，强韧豁免，可以叠加，目标的强韧豁免失去你的传奇智力点成功数。当目标因为该晶化点数进入重度不良状态时，其直接死亡，这是一个B级即死效果。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===========================================================================================================

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">威力值：</font><font face="宋体">16</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">A+4000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：迅捷动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font><font face="宋体">7点道力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">成分：姿势、言语</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：见下</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：自身</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：见下</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：需引导，引导无需动作，最大持续</font><font face="宋体">1分钟。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：只见洛轻轻手中有光芒在闪烁，它呈现出奇特的半透明状，时而象是蝉翼，时而宛若天上的雷光。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">朝着最先冲过来的气团，洛轻轻举起了手中的</font><font face="宋体">“剑”。她知道这是一个术。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当她寻得那个答案时，这个术便浮现在脑海之中，并且她瞬间理解了术的全部。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">用那个声音的话来说，这既是力量，也是代价。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">她这一生都将与秩序绑定在一起。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">一旦违背，便是瓦解。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">求之不得，洛轻轻心中说道，接着挥下利剑！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">刹那间，身边涌动的气回应了她的意志</font><font face="宋体">——</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">剑光刺破地面，并如裂隙一般向前冲出！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这一剑仿佛劈开了大地！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">她身前的数十尺范围，皆在刃锋斩击范围之内。冲在最前面的壮汉还未靠近她身边五步距离，肩膀处便已断开，巨大的裂口一直延伸至腰间！</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你获得传奇决心</font><font face="宋体">/柄龙鳞剑，你可以以一个自由动作，控制一柄龙鳞剑发动一次攻击，同一柄龙鳞剑在一回合内只能攻击一次。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">龙鳞剑有两种不同的攻击方式，一种是对一个目标进行一次远程施法攻击，射程为智力值</font><font face="宋体">*10米，造成穿刺严重伤害；另外一种是进行一次施法检定，对半径为决心值*2米的球形范围内的所有敌对目标造成施法检定成功数/点伤害，所有受影响的目标反射豁免，射程为触及。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：触及</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：一个目标</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：</font><font face="宋体">24小时</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：按照秘录上的描述，这门仙术施展时无声、无光，如果对气的敏锐程度不高，甚至很难察觉到有人发起了攻击。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">而它的效果也十分诡异。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">施术者可以自行控制术法威力，当投入的气较多时，此术类似于离法，能引发灼烧与火焰。并且它的高温不仅仅聚集于表面，还能直接伤及目标内部，无论是盔甲还是衣物都无法阻挡。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">若降低气的消耗，它几乎没有直接效果，但在数天之后，中术者同样会感到灼烧带来的剧痛，身体也会溃烂腐败，宛若遭到恶疾侵蚀一般。更关键的是，大多数治疗手段都对其无效，哪怕方士自身的恢复能力再强，最终都难逃过一死。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">秘录的最后还提到，此术虽然防不胜防，施展距离却极短，只有在两步范围内才能达到理想效果，超过这个距离时，仙术的威力将会直线下降。故此枢密府为其起了个贴切的名字：九幽火。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">然而在夏凡看来，该术倒更象是一种</font><font face="宋体">……辐射。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你对目标进行一次远程施法攻击，造成光能严重伤害。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">若成功命中，则你令目标在其每回合开始时，都受到你的（传奇智力</font><font face="宋体">+科学技能等级带来的附加成功）点光能严重伤害。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你以该法术造成的伤害，可以无视目标的任何伤害降低能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续期间，任何治疗效果（包括快速医疗）均对目标无效。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">本法术是一个</font><font face="宋体">A级诅咒效果。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===========================================================================================================
